控部门、风险管理责任部门、内审部门及各分支机构构成,并建立了包括政策制度、管理办法、
操作细则、规范性文件在内的四层级制度体系。公司董事会负责建立和保持有效的全面风险管理
体系，承担风险管理的最终责任。高级管理层负责制定风险管理政策和程序，承担全面风险管理
的实施责任。高级管理层下设信用风险审查委员会、资产负债管理委员会等专业委员会，并指定
各类风险主控部门及管理部门。针对信用风险、市场风险、操作风险等各类风险，公司制定了相
应的风险管理政策及程序，建设上线信用风险、操作风险、流动性风险等风险管理系统，明确了
各类风险识别、计量、监测、缓释及报告流程，确保各类风险能够准确识别、有效处置。其中，10公司采用权重法计量信用风险加权资产及资本要求，采用标准法计量市场风险加权资产及资本要
求，采用基本指标法计量操作风险加权资产及资本要求。2020年，公司严格按照董事会工作部
署，坚持以高质量稳健发展为中心，不断健全全面风险管理体系，持续完善风险管理制度流程，
升级优化相关风险管理系统，扎实推动风控措施落地落实，实现业务产品全面覆盖、制度流程全
程控制、风险防控全员参与，保障了各项业务持续稳健发展。
（一）信用风险及对策
信用风险是指债务人或交易对手未能履行合同规定的义务或信用质量发生变化，影响金融产
品价值，从而给公司造成经济损失的风险。报告期内，公司从以下方面加强信用风险管理：一是
夯实信贷管理基础。制定信贷条线工作指导意见，明确年度工作思路、工作目标及具体措施，修
订完善信贷管理基本制度，简化优化各项业务操作流程，全面提升信贷管理工作质效。二是推行
信贷精细化管理。制定2020年授信政策指引，全面推行授信项目限时办结、延伸审查和后评价，
扎实推动放款审核规范化管理，不断提升分层次贷后管理效能，严防新增信用风险。三是强化信
贷管理科技赋能。以对公信贷作业流程为主线，建设上线信贷业务科技赋能项目，涵盖智准营
销、智信尽调、智汇风控等五大引擎，不断提升客户经理获客能力、作业标准化和风控水平。四
是优化信用风险管理系统。升级优化信用风险管理系统，顺利完成系统框架信息安全升级、评级
模型优化、评级流程再造等工作，进一步健全非零售与零售内部评级体系，严把授信准入关口。
五是持续开展资产质量攻坚。按照“尊重历史、着眼当前、充分反映、积极处置”原则，制定信
用风险处置化解方案和责任划段管理台账，按月倒排工期，积极化解存量，全面提升信贷资产处
置质量。
（二）市场风险及对策
市场风险是指因市场价格（利率、汇率、股票价格和商品价格）的不利变动，从而使银行表
内外业务发生损失的风险。报告期内，公司从以下方面加强市场风险管理：一是建立指标监测预
警机制。健全市场利率信息收集、反馈机制，逐日监控市场信用违约情况，按季监测利率敏感性
指标，及时采取措施消除风险隐患。二是不断强化限额管理。制定市场风险偏好策略，明确资金
交易限额、债券投资限额、交易性债券止损限额阈值，密切监测各类限额政策执行情况，确保单
一限额、日累计限额符合限额管理要求。三是持续加大资金业务风险管控。合理配置短期资产，
适当投资货币基金，不断提升短期资金利用率及收益水平，规避市场波动带来的利率风险。建设
上线新版资金业务管理系统，全面分析交易品种、投资组合和账户信息，为资金投资提供决策依
据。四是加强银行账户利率风险管理。在对国内宏观经济、财政政策进行研究分析基础上，科学
研判未来存贷款利率走势，不断完善产品定价管理系统，健全客户定价模型，实现以客户综合价
值评价为基础的定价测算。五是有效规范汇率风险管理。制定贸易金融业务定价精细化方案，修11订外汇资金定价管理办法，优化代客结售汇汇率定价机制，并实行外汇交易逐级授权，有效防范
汇率风险。(三)操作风险及对策操作风险是指由不完善或有问题的内部控制程序、员工、信息科技系统以及外部事件所造
成损失的风险。报告期内，公司从以下方面加强操作风险管理：一是组织开展“合规文化深化
年”。制定“合规文化深化年”实施方案，扎实开展合规规制、合规执行、合规监督、合规整纠
等环节建设，并举办合规政策及文化宣讲、合规征文及主题演讲等活动，努力构建“令行禁止、
照章办事、知行合一、主动合规”的合规文化。二是持续深化制度流程建设。制定《莱商银行制
度管理办法》，建立制度制定、执行、监督、评估、维护的全流程闭环管理机制，有效规范制度
建设与管理。同时修订完善内控合规“一图两表”、押品评估管理办法等制度流程，为全员合规
操作提供简洁、实用的指导手册。三是全面开展内控检查排查。制定年度内控合规与操作风险检
查排查计划，推动完成重点领域检查排查，并对分行开展飞行检查，及时发现和纠正可能存在的
操作风险隐患。四是持续强化案件防控管理。全面推行案防工作目标管理责任制，修订完善案件
防控工作管理办法、员工违规行为处罚办法等制度，并组织开展员工行为排查和案防知识学习测
试等工作，进一步提升全行案件防控管理水平。(四)流动性风险及对策流动性风险是指公司无法以合理成本及时获得充足资金，用于偿付到期债务、履行其他支
付义务和满足正常业务开展的其他资金需求的风险。报告期内，公司从以下方面加强流动性风险
管理：一是不断加强流动性监测预警。借助资产负债管理系统，加强流动性比例、流动性缺口率
等指标监测预警，及时采取措施消除风险隐患，确保流动性合理充裕。密切关注货币市场资金走
势，认真做好月末、节假日、缴税期等时点资金计划与安排，保障特殊时点支付安全。二是调整
优化资产负债结构。负债端，通过调整定期存款FTP定价策略、加大存单推广发行力度等措施，
不断提高负债来源多元化和稳定性。资产端，积极调整优化投资业务结构，合理配置资产到期期
限，持续压降自营投资规模，适当增持国债、政策债等优质资产，实现流动性充足。三是持续深
化应急能力建设。按季开展流动性压力测试，科学设置流动性压力测试情景，重点测试存款流失
情境下流动性风险承受能力，修正完善流动性应急预案，进一步提升流动性风险识别、监测、预
警和处置能力。（五）信息科技风险及对策信息科技风险是指信息科技在银行运用过程中，由于自然因素、人为因素、技术漏洞和管理
缺陷产生的操作、法律和声誉等风险。报告期内，公司从以下方面加强信息科技风险管理：一是12不断完善信息科技治理体系。修订完善信息科技管理委员会工作规则，定期召开信息科技管理委
员会会议，并扎实开展信息科技管理制度宣讲，信息科技治理体系不断完善。二是持续加强基础
设施建设。制定年度信息科技基础建设规划，顺利完成同城灾备网络优化完善、虚拟化平台版本
升级等工作，并组织开展数据中心基础设施隐患排查，不断增强信息科技系统运行稳定性。三是
逐步提高网络安全管理能力。组织开展非授权软件风险排查和电子设备漏洞检测等工作，搭建数
据信息保护系统和态势感知数据上报平台，不断提升数据信息安全防范能力。四是持续加大信息
安全保护力度。印发《信息安全月报》，组织开展客户信息保护专项培训、信息安全专项整治活
动、信息科技安全巡查等工作，进一步提升信息安全水平。五是不断增强业务连续性管理能力。
修订完善业务连续性管理委员会工作规则和办法，制定年度业务连续性计划，建设完成异地数据
级灾备中心，组织开展各类演练，进一步提升全行业务连续性管理能力。十、内部控制评价公司高度重视内部控制体系建设，严格遵循全覆盖、制衡性、审慎性及相匹配原则，不断健
全内控管理架构，持续完善内控管理机制，及时修订内控管理制度流程，并扎实推动各项内控管
理措施落地实施。通过对内控体系建设、内控措施实施和内控运行结果进行系统性调查、测试、
分析和评估，公司内部控制体系从内部控制环境、风险识别与评估、内部控制措施与执行、内
部检查监督、信息交流与反馈等方面，基本涵盖了所有业务、产品、渠道、管理及其关键环节等
内控要素，内部控制体系基本健全，流程设置科学合理，在完善公司治理体系、推动全行转型发
展、创新创优业务产品、防范化解风险等方面得到了有效执行。十一、内部审计情况公司内部审计工作由董事会领导、监事长分管，确保了审计的独立性。公司设立了内审部，
负责对经营管理、内部控制、风险管理、财务管理、薪酬管理及管理人员履职等事项进行审计，
向董事会和下设的审计委员会负责并报告工作，接受监事会监督和指导。
报告期内，公司围绕发展中心和战略部署，严格落实监管要求，实施以风险为导向的审计活
动，将业务合规性、风险和内部控制隐患作为审计监督主线和检查重点，完善审计管理机制，加
强审计信息化建设，拓展审计监督广度和深度，全面落实年度审计计划，突出对主要分支机构、
重点业务领域、操作流程、关键环节及重要岗位人员的审计监督，并加强对审计发现问题整改工
作的跟踪与督导，有效发挥内部审计的监督、评价和咨询作用，助推风险管理、内部控制和公司
治理水平持续提升，为公司的稳健经营和高质量发展提供有力保障。13Chapter II Summary of Accounting Data and Business DataI. Major profit indicators during the reporting periodUnit: RMB 1,000.00Item20202019Operating IncomeTotal ProfitNet Profit Attributed to the Parent Company's

after AdjustmentLeverage Ratio %12,800,633.7010,188,195.50200,738,685.80176,313,267.906.38%5.78%IX. Various Risks and Risk Management of the CompanyThe Company’s comprehensive risk management system is composed of the Board of Directors, the 
Board of Supervisors, senior management, the Comprehensive Risk Management Department, the Main 
Risk Management Control Department, the Risk Management Responsibility Department, the Internal 
Audit Department and their branches, and has established a four-tier system including policy system, 
management measures, operation rules and normative documents. The Board of Directors is responsible 
for establishing and maintaining an effective and comprehensive risk management system and ultimately 
for risk management.  The senior management is responsible for formulating the risk management policies 
and procedures and for implementing comprehensive risk management. The senior management has set18up special committees such as the Credit Risk Review Committee and the Assets-Liabilities Management 
Committee, and also designated the main control departments and management departments of various 
risks. The company has formulated the corresponding risk management policies and procedures for 
various risks such as credit risk, market risk and operation risk, built an online management information 
system for credit risk, operation risk and liquidity risk, and specified various types of risk identification, 
measurement, monitoring, mitigation and reporting processes to ensure that various risks can be accurately 
identified and effectively disposed, that is, the Company has taken the weighting method to measure 
credit risk weighted assets and capital requirements, the standard method to measure market risk weighted 
assets and capital requirements, and the basic index method to measure operation risk weighted assets and 
capital requirements. In 2020, in strict accordance with the work arrangement of the Board of Directors, 
the Company adhered to the high-quality and steady development as her central task, keep improving 
the comprehensive risk management system and the risk management institutional process flow, upgrade 
and optimize relevant risk management systems, promote taking risk control measures, basically achieve 
comprehensive coverage of business product, exercise full control over the system process, and fully 
participate in risk prevention and control, thus ensuring the sustained and steady development of each 
business.(i) Credit Risks and Their CountermeasuresCredit risk means the risk of economic loss to the Company caused by influence on the value of 
financial product resulted from failure to fulfill obligations stipulated in the contract of or change of 
credit quality of debtors or counterparties. During the reporting period, the Company strengthened credit 
risk management from the following aspects: first, consolidated the foundation of credit management;  
formulate guidance on the work of credit line, clarify the annual work considerations, work objectives 
and specific measures, revise and improve the basic credit management system, simplify and optimize 
all business operation processes, and comprehensively improve the quality and efficiency of credit 
management; secondly, implemented meticulous credit management: formulated credit policy guidelines 
of 2020, fully implemented the regulations of time-limited completion, extended review and post-
evaluation of credit projects, solidly promote standardized management of loan review, keep improving 
the efficiency of post-loan management at different levels, and strictly control new credit risks; thirdly, 
strengthened the technological empowerment of credit management: taking the corporate credit operation 
process as the main line, build a technology empowerment project for online credit business, covering 
five engines, such as intelligent accurate marketing, intelligent due diligence and intelligent risk control, 
keep improving the customer acquisition skill, operation standardization and risk control of account 
managers; fourthly, optimized the credit risk management system: upgraded and optimized the credit risk 
management system, successfully completed  information security upgrade of the system framework, 
rating model optimization, rating process re-engineering and the like work, further improved the non-
retail and retail internal rating system, and strictly controlled the credit access threshold;  fifthly, continued 
tackling key problems in asset quality:  formulated solutions to credit risk disposition and resolution and 
a responsibility division management ledger on the principle of "respect for history, focus on the present, 
fully reflection and actively disposal", back-schedule the time for completion on a monthly basis, actively 
resolve the stock, and comprehensively improve the disposal quality of credit asset.(ii) Market Risks and Their Countermeasures19Market Risk means the risks of loss to the Bank’s business activities on and off the balance sheet due 
to any adverse change in market price (interest rate, exchange rate, share price and commodity price). 
During the reporting period, the Company strengthened market risk management from the following 
aspects: first, established an index monitoring and early warning mechanism: improve the market interest 
rate information collection and feedback mechanism, monitor market credit default on a daily basis, 
monitor interest rate sensitivity indicators quarterly, and take timely measures to eliminate potential risk; 
secondly, continuously strengthen quota management: formulate a market risk preference strategy, specify 
the threshold of capital trading limit, bond investment limit and tradable bond stop loss limit, closely 
monitor the implementation of all limit policies, and ensure that the single limit and daily cumulative limit 
meet the limit management requirement; thirdly, continued increasing risk control of capital business: 
reasonably allocated short-term assets, appropriately invested in monetary fund, made continuous 
improvement of short-term fund utilization rate and income level to avoid interest rate risks caused by 
market fluctuations; built a new online fund business management system to comprehensively analyze 
transaction varieties, investment portfolios and account information to provide decision-making basis 
for fund investment; fourthly, strengthened interest rate risk management in bank account: scientifically 
judged the future trend of deposit and loan interest rate on the basis of research and analysis of domestic 
macro-economic and fiscal policies of China, made continuous improvement of product pricing 
management system, improved the customer pricing model, and realized pricing calculation based on 
customer comprehensive value evaluation; fifthly, effectively regulated exchange rate risk management:  
made a refined pricing plan for trade finance business, revised the pricing management measures for 
foreign exchange fund, optimized the exchange rate pricing mechanism for settlement and sale of foreign 
exchange on behalf of customers, and implemented step-by-step authorization for foreign exchange 
transactions to effectively prevent exchange rate risk.(iii) Operational Risks and Their CountermeasuresOperational risk is defined as the risk of loss resulting from inadequate or failed internal control 
processes, personnel and IT systems or from external event. During the reporting period, the Company 
strengthened operational risk management from the following aspects: first, organized the campaign of 
"Year of Deepening Compliance Culture": formulated the implementation plan of the "Year of Deepening 
Compliance Culture", constructed compliance regulation, compliance implementation, compliance 
supervision, compliance rectification and so on in a down-to-earth manner, and hold activities such as 
compliance policy and culture publicity, solicitation of articles or essays on compliance and keynote 
speeches to build a compliance culture of "executing orders and proclaim prohibition, acting according 
to regulations, integrating knowledge and practice, and active compliance with regulations"; secondly, 
continued deepening construction of institutional processes: formulated the Measures for the System 
Management of Laishang Bank, established a closed-loop management mechanism for the full process of 
system formulation, implementation, supervision, evaluation and maintenance, and effectively standardize 
the system construction and management, revise and improve systems and processes of internal control 
and compliance such as "one blueprint of planning, one time schedule and one execution program", 
collateral evaluation management measures and so on to provide concise and practical instructions 
for all compliance operations; thirdly, launched internal control inspection and investigation in an all-
round way: made an annual internal control compliance and operational risk inspection and investigation20plan, promoted the completion of inspection and investigation in key areas such as enterprise finance, 
trade finance and retail, and make a spot  inspection on branches to discover and correct possible 
operational risks in time; fourthly, continued strengthening case prevention and control management: 
fully implemented the target management responsibility system for case prevention, revised and improved 
management measures for case prevention and control and punishment measures for employee’s violation, 
and organized the investigation on employee’s behaviors and study and test of case prevention knowledge 
so as to further improve the management of case prevention and control throughout the Bank.(iv) Liquidity Risks and Their CountermeasuresThe liquidity risk means the risk that a commercial bank is unable to acquire sufficient capital in 
time with reasonable cost to discharge matured debts, perform other obligations of payment and meet 
other demand of capital for normal operation of business. During the reporting period, the Company 
strengthened liquidity risk management from the following aspects: first, continuously strengthened 
liquidity monitoring and early warning:  strengthened the monitoring and early warning of indicators such 
as liquidity ratio and liquidity gap rate with the help of the asset and liability management system, and 
took timely measures to eliminate potential risk to ensure reasonable and abundant liquidity, paid close 
attention to the trend of capital in the monetary market, earnestly planned and arranged capital in the end 
of each month, holidays, tax payment periods and other time points to ensure the safety of payment at 
special time points; secondly, adjusted and optimized the structure of assets and liabilities:  on the side of 
liabilities, continuously improved the diversification and stability of liability source by adjusting the FTP 
pricing strategy of time deposit and increasing the promotion and issuance of certificate of deposit; on the 
side of assets, actively adjusted and optimized the investment business structure, rationally allocated the 
maturity of assets, continuously reduced the scale of proprietary investment, and appropriately increase 
the holding of high-quality assets such as treasury bonds and policy bonds to achieve sufficient liquidity; 
thirdly, continued deepening construction of emergency response capacity: performed liquidity stress test 
quarterly, scientifically set liquidity stress test scenarios, focused on test liquidity risk tolerance under 
deposit loss scenarios, revised and improved liquidity emergency response plans, and further enhanced 
liquidity risk identification, monitoring, early warning and disposal capabilities.(v) IT Risks and Their CountermeasuresThe IT risk means the Bank’s operational, legal and reputational risk arising from natural factors, 
artificial factors, technology bug and management flaw in the application of IT. During the reporting 
period, the Company strengthened information technology risk management from the following aspects: 
first, continuously improved the information technology governance system: revised and improved the 
rules of procedure of the Information Technology Management Committee, hold regular meetings of 
the Information Technology Management Committee, and carried out solid publicity on the information 
technology management system, and continuously improved the information technology governance 
system;  secondly, continued strengthening infrastructure construction:  made the annual information 
technology infrastructure plan, successfully completed the optimization and improvement of local 
disaster preparedness network, upgraded the version of virtualization platform, etc., and organized the 
investigation of hidden trouble in data center infrastructure to continuously enhance the operational 
stability of information technology systems; thirdly, gradually improved the network security management 
capability:  organized risk screening of unauthorized software and vulnerability detection of electronic21equipment, built a data information protection system and a situational awareness data reporting platform, 
and continuously improved the ability of data information security; fourthly, continued strengthening 
information security protection: issued the Information Security Monthly Report, organized and delivered 
special training on customer information protection, special rectification activities on information security, 
information technology security inspection and the like to further improve information security; fifthly, 
continuously enhanced business continuity management capabilities: revised and improved the working 
rules and methods of the Business Continuity Management Committee, made the annual business 
continuity plan, built and completed the remote data-level disaster recovery center, organized all drills 
required, and further enhanced the business continuity management capability of the entire bank.X. Evaluation of Internal ControlThe Company attached great importance to construction of internal control system strictly on the 
principles of full coverage, checks and balances, prudence and matching, made continuous improvement 
of internal control management structure and internal control management mechanism, timely revised the 
internal control management system process, and solidly promoted taking all internal control management 
measures. Through systematic investigation, test, analysis and evaluation of internal control system 
construction, internal control measures and internal control operation result, the Company's internal 
control system, in terms of internal control environment, risk identification and evaluation, internal control 
measures and implementation, internal inspection and supervision, information exchange and feedback, 
has basically covered all internal control elements such as business, product, channel, management and 
their key processes; the internal control system is basically perfected and the process setting is scientific 
and reasonable, and have been effectively implemented in improving the corporate governance system, 
promoting the transformation and development of the entire bank, innovating and creating excellent 
business product, avoiding and resolving risks.XI. Internal AuditThe Company’s internal audit is under the leadership of the Board of Directors and in the 
responsibility of the Chief Supervisor to ensure the independence of the audit. This Bank has set up an 
internal audit department, which is responsible for auditing operation management, internal control, risk 
management, financial management, payroll management and performance of duties by management, 
responsible and reporting to the Board of Directors, subject to the guidance of the Board of Supervisors 
and inspection, supervision and evaluation of the audit committee;During the reporting period, focus on the development center and strategic deployment in strict 
compliance with regulatory requirement, launch risk-oriented audit activities, take business compliance, 
risk and hidden danger of internal control as the main line of audit and supervision and the focus of 
inspection, improve the audit management mechanism, strengthen the informatization construction of 
audit, expand the breadth and depth of audit supervision, fully implement the annual audit plan, highlight 
the audit supervision on major branches, key business areas, operational processes, key processes 
and personnel on important positions, and strengthen the tracking and supervision on the rectification 
of problems found in audit, effectively play the role of supervision, evaluation and consultation of 
internal audit, promote the continuous improvement of risk management, internal control and corporate 
governance, and provide a strong guarantee for the steady operation and high-quality development of the 
Company.22第三章 股本变动及股东情况一、股本变动情况截至报告期末，公司股东总数2201个，公司股本结构如下：（单位：股）项目法人股自然人股合计2020年12月31日2019年12月31日2,808,006,956.00191,993,044.003,000,000,000.002,807,426,956.00192,573,044.003,000,000,000.00二、股东情况报告期末，公司前十名股东持股情况如下表：序

and the related transaction management of the enterprise accounting standards, the Company, in accordance 
with different definitions of the related parties based on different regulatory requirements, classified and 
identified the related parties and regularly updated and identified the list of related parties.The related transaction business between the Company and related parties is the normal business 
requirement of the Company, and the general provisions of the Company's business management and 
regulatory agencies are implemented for the transaction conditions and pricing levels, without any 
circumstance better than the general borrower or counterparty. The business procedures also comply with 
the related provisions of the regulatory authorities and the Company's related transaction management.During the reporting period, the Company's related transactions are mainly in-balance-sheet and off-
balance-sheet credit businesses provided for the related party and the capital transactions occurring in the 
related party. All related transactions are performed normally, without any negative effect on the Company's 
operating results and financial conditions.36(i) Related Party's Profile

At the end of the reporting period, the maximum credit granting balance for a single affiliated party 
was RMB 0.5 billion, accounting for 3.5% of the total net capital of the Bank; that for a single related 
legal person or group client to which the other organization belongs was RMB 1.183 billiom, accounting 
for 8.32% of the total net capital of the Bank; the total credit granting balance for all affiliated parties 
was RMB 4.061billion, accounting for 28.57% of the total net capital of the Bank, all of which met the 
regulatory requirements.47第四章  董事、监事、高级管理人员和员工情况

1.薪酬管理架构及决策程序
公司建立了科学的薪酬管理架构，明确规定董事、监事的报酬由股东大会决定,董事会决定
高级管理人员的报酬。董事会对公司薪酬管理负最终责任，负责审阅、批准、修订公司薪酬管理
制度与政策、薪酬成本与预算等，监督公司薪酬制度实施情况，并定期评估公司薪酬机制的健全
性和有效性。董事会下设提名与薪酬考核委员会，负责审议有关薪酬制度、政策及监督工作。高
级管理层负责实施董事会薪酬管理方面的决议，组织制定并更新公司薪酬管理制度与政策，管理
和控制薪酬预算与成本，审阅、批准员工的定薪、调薪方案、绩效考核方案、员工福利方案等。
（公司纳入济南市市属国有企业负责人范围的高级管理人员，其薪酬由济南市国资委牵头考核确
定；公司其他高级管理人员的薪酬由董事会和下设的提名与薪酬考核委员会根据董事会制订的薪
酬考核办法考核确定。）收入11785万元。2.年度薪酬总额、受益人与结构分布情况
2020年，公司薪酬总额为61575万元，薪酬结构分布如下：

4.薪酬延期支付和非现金薪酬情况，包括因故扣回的情况。
公司建立了绩效薪酬的延期支付机制，根据员工不同层级及岗位差异，对各级管理人员以及
对风险有重要影响岗位上的员工的绩效薪酬实行延期支付，并设定延期支付时间及支付比例，对
延期追索及扣回的情形均做了特别的规定说明。现，分支行绩效工资按照《莱商银行绩效考核管理办法》进行考核后兑现。515.薪酬政策
公司薪酬制度遵循“市场导向、岗位导向、绩效导向、能力导向”的付薪理念，于2016年开
展了薪酬体系优化设计项目，根据员工岗位职责及标准进行人岗匹配，实行了以岗定薪、按月拨
付的固定薪酬制度，将薪酬总额与全行经营利润挂钩，建立自上而下的薪酬总额挂钩经营利润的
提取机制，以及自下而上的薪酬总额核算机制，逐步健全全行薪酬总额管控机制。
根据监管要求并结合公司实际，公司制定了《莱商银行薪酬管理办法》《莱商银行绩效薪酬
延期支付管理办法》，上述制度已经公司职工代表大会审议通过。
公司薪酬实行统一管理、分级实施的管理体系，并致力于建设科学合理的薪酬管理体系。董
事会按照国家有关法律和政策确定公司的薪酬管理制度和政策，并对薪酬管理负最终责任。董事
会设立提名与薪酬考核委员会，由独立董事担任主任。高级管理层负责履行薪酬管理职责，总行
人力资源部、计划财务部等部门负责执行薪酬政策，内审部负责对薪酬政策执行情况进行监督。

7.超出原定薪酬方案的例外情况

DirectorVice PresidentDirectorSupervisor(vi) Remunerations Structure of the Company1. Remunerations Management Structure and Decision-making Procedure
The company has established a scientific remuneration management structure, clearly stipulating that 
the remuneration of directors and supervisors shall be decided by the general meeting of shareholders, 
and the Board of Directors shall decide the remuneration of senior managers. The Board of Directors 
is ultimately responsible for the salary management of the Bank, responsible for reviewing, approving, 
revising the remuneration management system and policies, and remuneration cost and budget of the 
Bank, supervising the implementation of the Bank's remuneration system, and regularly assessing 
the soundness and effectiveness of the remuneration mechanism. Under the Board of Directors is 
the Nomination and Remuneration Assessment Committee, which is responsible for reviewing work 
relating to the remuneration system, policy and supervision. Senior management is responsible for the 
implementation of resolutions of the Board of Directors about the remuneration management, organizing 
to develop and update the remuneration management system and policies, managing and controlling 
salary budget and cost, reviewing and approving the employees' wage fixing and salary increase plan, 
performance appraisal plan and staff benefit plan, etc. (The remuneration of the senior managers of the 
Company incorporated in the scope of the heads of state-owned enterprises in Jinan shall be determined 
by the department of SASAC, and the remuneration of other senior managers of the Company shall be 
determined following the nomination by the Board of Directors and evaluation based on the remuneration 
appraisal methods formulated by the remuneration appraisal committee and the Board of Directors.)2. Total Annual Remuneration, Beneficiary and Structure Distribution
In 2020, the total remuneration of the Company was RMB615.75 million, with its structuredistribution as follows:RMB209.03 million of fixed compension,accounting for 33.95% of the total amount;RMB288.87 
million of variable compension,accounting for 46.91% of the total amount;RMB117.85 million of welfare 
income such as Five Insurance & Two Funds ect.,accounting for 19.14% of the total amount.3. The standard of remunerations and performance measurement and risk adjustment
Performance salary of the department/office employees of the Company's head office shall be paid 
based on appraisal according to the provisions of the Management Measures for Performance Appraisal of56Department/Office of Laishang Bank's Head Office, and that of branch employees based on the provisions 
of the Management Measures for Performance Appraisal of Laishang Bank.4. Deferred payment of remunerations and non-cash remunerations, including deduction for somereason.The Bank has established a deferred payment mechanism for performance salary and implemented 
deferred payment of performance salary for managers at all levels and employees in positions that have 
a significant impact on risks, according to different levels of employees and position differences, and set 
up the deferred payment time and payment ratio and made special provisions on the circumstances of 
deferred claims and deductions.
5. Policy of remunerations 
The remuneration system of the Company conforms to the payment concept of the "market-oriented, 
post-oriented, performance-oriented, capability-oriented" principle. In 2016, the Company carried out the 
optimization and design program for the remuneration system, implemented a fixed remuneration system 
on a monthly basis according to the staff's post responsibilities and standards of person-to-job matching, 
linked the total remuneration to the operating profit throughout the Bank, established a top-down 
withdrawal mechanism with total remuneration linked to the operating profit as well as bottom-up total 
remuneration accounting mechanism, and gradually improved the management and control mechanism 
for total remuneration throughout the Bank.In accordance with the regulatory requirements and combined with the actual situation, the Company 
has formulated the Measures for the Administration of Remuneration of Laishang Bank and the Measures 
for the Administration of Deferred Payment of Performance Remuneration of Laishang Bank, which has 
been deliberated and adopted by the Company's Staff Congress.The  Company's  remuneration  adopts  uniformly  managed  and  hierarchically  implemented 
management system, and is dedicated to building a scientific and reasonable remuneration management 
system. The Board of Directors determines the Company's remuneration management system and policy 
according to the relevant laws and policies of the country, and is ultimately responsible for remuneration 
management. The Board of Directors sets up the nomination and Remuneration Assessment Committee, 
and independent director acts as the director of the committee. Senior management is responsible for 
remuneration management, and the HR Department, Financial Planning Department of the headquarter 
are responsible for implementing the remuneration policy and Internal Audit Department is responsible 
for supervising the implementation process.6. Preparation of annual remuneration plan and completion of assessment
The Company's annual remuneration plan was prepared according to the size of staff, business 
development, etc. In 2020, various operational indicators of the Company were good, and the 
remunerations reasonably reflected the performance and risk management of the Company.7. Exceptions beyond the original remunerations plan
There was no exception beyond the original remunerations plan in the Company during the reportingperiod.II. Profile of EmployeesAt the end of the reporting period, there were 2,326 employees on duty in the Company, including2023with undergraduate or above degree, accounting for 86.97%.57第五章 公司治理结构
一、公司治理情况报告期内，公司严格遵守《公司法》和《商业银行法》的有关规定，认真落实监管部门关于
公司治理的有关规定，致力于进一步完善公司治理结构，增强公司治理机制的有效性，提高董事
会决策的科学性。公司治理具体情况如下：
（一）关于股东与股东大会。公司按照《公司章程》和《股东大会议事规则》的要求召集、
召开股东大会，积极听取股东的意见和建议，确保股东对公司重大事项的知情权、参与权和表决
权。报告期内，公司召开了2019年度股东大会、2020年第一次临时股东大会、2020年第二次临
时股东大会，会议严格按照有关规定履行了相关法律程序，保证了股东参会并行使权利，并由律
师出具了法律意见书。
（二）关于董事和董事会。公司现有董事9名，其中独立董事3名。董事会能够严格按照《公
司章程》的规定，认真履行职责，在股东大会授权下进行决策，强化公司治理，推进战略步伐，
促进稳健经营，维护了公司和全体股东的利益。报告期内公司共召开了6次董事会会议。
目前，公司董事会下设1个办公室和6个专门委员会，包括董事会办公室、关联交易控制委员
会、风险管理委员会、战略发展委员会、审计委员会、提名与薪酬考核委员会、消费者权益保护
委员会，其中风险管理委员会下设声誉风险管理专业委员会和信息科技风险管理专业委员会。6
个专门委员会具有明确的职权范围，监管公司不同方面的事务，并对董事会负责，为董事会决策
提供了建设性建议，进一步提高了董事会决策的科学性。
（三）关于监事和监事会。公司现有监事9人，其中职工监事3人，外部监事3人。监事会按
照《公司章程》的规定认真履行职责，对公司财务、风险管理、资产质量以及部分高级管理人员
履职的合规性进行监督检查，定期及不定期地与外部审计机构和管理层进行情况交流，有针对性
地开展专项检查，针对风险隐患和发现的问题，向董事会和管理层提出建议和改进意见，从而更
加有效地发挥监事会的作用。报告期内公司共召开了5次监事会会议。
（四）关于信息披露与透明度。公司在《金融时报》和公司网站发布了《2019年度报告》，
并制作了《莱商银行股份有限公司2019年度报告》（摘要）单行本，及时准确地进行信息披露，
切实维护广大股东特别是中小投资者的利益。 
二、独立董事及履行职责情况报告期内，公司董事会现有独立董事3人，独立董事本着为全体股东负责的态度，履行诚信
和勤勉义务，认真参加董事会及各专门委员会会议，积极发表意见，维护公司整体利益及中小股
东的合法权益不受侵犯。58（一）独立董事参加会议情况。报告期内，独立董事应参加董事会会议18人次，亲自出席18
（二）独立董事对公司有关事项提出异议情况。报告期内，公司独立董事未对公司本年度董人次，委托出席0人次，缺席0人次。
事会的议案提出异议。
三、外部监事及履行职责情况报告期内，公司监事会现有外部监事3人，外部监事本着为全体股东负责的态度，履行诚信
和勤勉义务，认真参加监事会及各专门委员会会议，积极发表意见，维护公司整体利益及中小股
东的合法权益不受侵犯。
（一）外部监事参加会议情况。报告期内，公司监事应参加监事会会议15人次，亲自出席14
人次，委托出席1人次，缺席0人次。
（二）外部监事对公司有关事项提出异议情况。报告期内，公司外部监事未对公司本年度董
事会、监事会的议案提出异议。
四、公司经营决策体系公司最高权力机构是股东大会，通过董事会、监事会进行管理和监督。行长受聘于董事会，
对公司日常经营管理全面负责。公司实行一级法人体制，各分支机构均为非独立核算单位，其经
营管理活动根据公司授权进行，并对公司负责。 
公司无控股股东。公司与大股东在业务、人员、资产、机构、财务五方面完全独立。公司具
有独立完整的业务及自主经营能力，董事会、监事会和内部机构能够独立运作。
五、高级管理人员考评及激励机制报告期内，公司董事会制定了对高级管理人员的绩效考核管理办法，建立了薪酬与公司效益
和个人业绩相联系的激励约束机制；考核实行百分制，根据各高管人员的工作性质不同，考核项
目有所侧重。对于非执行董事、非职工监事的考核主要以其出席会议次数及履职能力考核为主。
制定了《莱商银行股份有限公司董事会董事履职评价制度》，主要分为客观评价、自我评价和相
互评价三个部分，根据各项指标具体内容的不同，给予不同的比重。公司制定了《莱商银行股份
有限公司董事会对高管人员履职评价办法》《莱商银行股份有限公司监事会对董事、监事、高管
人员履职评价办法》《关于追究董事、监事及高管人员责任的规定》。公司监事会制定了《莱商
银行股份有限公司监事会对高管人员履职评价办法实施细则》，明确了监事会对高级管理人员的
履职评价，加大了履职问责力度。59六、部门及分支机构设置
（一）公司组织架构图信息科技风险管理专业委员会声誉风险管理专业委员会关联交易控制委员会风险管理委员会提名与薪酬考核员会战略发展委员会审计委员会消费者权益保护委员会信息科技管理委员会财务管理委员会资产负债管理委员会制度评审委员会风险与合规管理委员会股东大会董事会监事会监督委员会提名委员会内审部现场审计中心非现场审计中心高级管理层信用风险审查委员会不良信贷资产管理委员会创新管理委员会同业投资委员会业务连续性管理委员会企

照64Chapter V Corporate Governance StructureI. Corporate governance of the CompanyDuring the reporting period, the Company strictly observed the related provisions in the 
Company Law and the Law on Commercial Banks, conscientiously implemented the related 
regulations of the regulatory intuition on corporate governance, and was dedicated to further 
improving corporate governance structure, enhancing the effectiveness of the corporate governance 
mechanism and making the decision of the Board of Directors more scientific. The performance of 
the Company in its corporate governance is as follows:(i) Shareholders and shareholders' general meetingThe Company convened the shareholders' general meeting in accordance with the requirement 
of the Articles of Association and the Rules of Procedures for Shareholders' Meeting and actively 
listened to shareholders' opinion and suggestion to ensure that all shareholders have the right to 
know, to participate and to vote to the major events of the Company.During the reporting period, the 
Company held its 2019 annual shareholders' general meeting, and 2020 first interim shareholders' 
general meeting. and 2020 second interim share holders' generd meeting. The meetings went through 
related legal procedures in strict accordance with the related regulations to ensure that shareholders 
participate in the meetings and exercise their right. Also, legal opinion was issued by a lawyer.(ii) Directors and the Board of DirectorsCurrently, the Company has 9 directors, including 3 independent directors. The Board of 
Directors is able to conscientiously perform its duties in strict accordance with the provisions in the 
Articles of Association, make decisions with the authorization of the shareholders' general meeting, 
strengthen the corporate governance, advance strategic steps and promote steady operation which 
safeguarded the interests of the Company and all shareholders. During the reporting period, the 
Company held 6 board meetings totally.Currently, under the Board of Directors of the Company there is 1 office and 6 special 
committees, including the Office of Board of Directors, Related Transaction Control Committee, 
Risk Management Committee, Strategic Development Committee, Audit Committee, Nomination 
and Remuneration Assessment Committee and Consumer Rights Protection Committee. Under 
the Risk Management Committee are the Special Committee of Reputation Risk Management and 
Special Committee of IT Risk Management.These 6 special committees have specific scopes of 
power, supervise and manage the matters at different aspects, and are accountable to the Board of 
Directors. They provide constructive suggestions for the decision making of the Board of Directors 
further to improve the science of the decisions made by the Board of Directors.(iii) Supervisors and the Board of SupervisorsThe Company has 9 supervisors, including 3 employee supervisors and 3 external supervisors.
The Board of Supervisors conscientiously performs its duties in strict accordance with the65provisions in the Articles of Association, carries out supervision and inspection over the compliance 
of the Company's finance, risk management, asset quality and the duty performance of the senior 
management, communicates with the external audit units and management regularly or irregularly, 
conducts targeted special inspections, and puts forward suggestions and improvement opinions to 
the Board of Directors and the management according to hidden risks or problems discovered, so 
as to play the role of the Board of Supervisors more effectively. During the reporting period, the 
Company held 5 board of supervisors meetings totally.(iv) Information disclosure and transparencyThe Company published its 2019 Annual Report on Financial Times and its website, and 
prepared a separate edition of 2019 Annual Report of Laishang Co., Ltd. (Summary), to carry out 
information disclosure in a timely and accurate manner and safeguard the interests of shareholders, 
particularly medium and small shareholders.II. Independent Directors and Their Performance of DutiesDuring the reporting period, there were 3 independent directors on the Board of Directors. 
With an attitude of being responsible to all shareholders, these independent directors performed the 
obligation of integrity and diligence, earnestly participated in the board meetings and meetings of 
various special committees, and actively delivered their opinions to safeguard the collective interest 
of the Company and the legitimate rights and interest of medium and small shareholders.(i) Independent directors' presence in meetingsDuring the reporting period, the number of independent directors attending the board meetings 
should be 18, with presence in 18 persons, entrusted attendance in 0 persons, and absence in 0 
person.(ii) Objections of the independent directors to related affairs of the CompanyDuring the reporting period, the independent directors of the Company did not object to anyproposal of the Board of Directors of the current year.III. External Supervisors and Their Performance of DutiesThere were 3 external supervisors in the Board of Supervisors in the Company during the 
report period. With an attitude of being responsible to all shareholders, these external supervisors 
performed their duty of integrity and diligence, carefully participated in the meeting of the Board 
of Supervisors and all special committee meetings, positively gave opinions and prevent overall 
benefit of the Company and lawful rights and interests of medium and small shareholders from 
infringement.(i) Presence of external supervisors in meetingsDuring the reporting period, the number of the supervisors attending the Board of Supervisors 
Meeting should be 15, with presence in 14 persons, entrusted attendance in 1 person and absence in 
0 person.66(ii) Objection raised by the external supervisorsDuring the reporting period, the external supervisors of the Company did not raise objections 
to the proposals of the Board of Directors and Board of Supervisors of the Company of the current 
year.IV. Operation and decision-making system of the CompanyThe highest authority of the Company is the Shareholders' General Meeting, which is managed 
and supervised through the Board of Directors and the Board of Supervisors. The president, 
employed by the Board of Directors, is responsible for all daily operation and management of 
the Company. Only the head office of the Company is its legal person, and all branches and sub-
branches are non-independent accounting units, whose operation and management activities shall be 
carried out with the authorization of the Company and who shall be responsible for the Company.The Company has no controlling shareholder. The Company and its majority shareholders 
are completely independent in terms of business, personnel, assets, organization and finance. The 
Company has independent and complete business and independent operation ability, and the Board 
of Directors, the Board of Supervisors and internal organizations can operate independently.V.Assessment and Incentive Mechanism and System of Senior 
ManagementDuring the reporting period, the Board of Directors of the Company further improved the 
performance appraisal management methods for senior management, and established an incentive 
and restraint mechanism which associates remuneration with the Company's effectiveness and 
personal performance; A hundred-mark system for assessment; the assessment project has an 
emphasis based on the work nature of senior management. The assessment of non-executive 
directors and non-employee supervisors has mainly focused on their attendance on meetings 
and ability to perform their duties. The Evaluation System of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd. on Duty 
Performance of Directors of the Board of Directors, which includes three parts, i.e., objective 
evaluation, self-evaluation and mutual evaluation, has been prepared. Different proportions are 
given according to different contents of various indexes. The Measures of the Board of Directors 
of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd. on Assessment of Senior Management's Performance, the Measures of 
the Board of Supervisors of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd. on Assessment of Directors, Supervisors and 
Senior Management's Performance and the Provisions of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd. on Accountability 
of Directors, Supervisors and Senior Management have been formulated. Meanwhile, the Board of 
Supervisors further quantified the criteria of assessment, formulated the Implementing Rules of Duty 
Performance Assessment Method on Senior Management by the Board of Supervisors of Laishang 
Bank Co., Ltd., specified the duty performance assessment on senior management by the Board of 
Supervisors and strengthened the accountability of duty performance.67VI. Setup of Departments and Branch Organizations

The Company held three general meetings of shareholders during the reporting period, with the details asfollows:On April 25, 2020, the 2019 Annual Shareholders' General Meeting was held in the auditorium on the 
first floor of the comprehensive business building of the Company. 48 shareholders and authorized agents 
attended the meeting, representing 2,710,775,922 shares, accounting for 90.35% of the Company's total share 
capital. The Shareholders' General Meeting has deliberated and adopted the 2019 Annual Work Report of the 
Board of Directors of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the 2019 Annual Work Report of the Board of Supervisors 
of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on the 2019 Annual Audit Report of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the 2019 
Annual Financial Report and Profit Distribution Scheme of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on the 2020 
Annual Budget of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the 2019 Annual Report on the Implementation of the Insider and 
Shareholder-related Transactions of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the 2019 Annual Report on Comprehensive 
Risk Management of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on Measures for Equity Trust of Laishang Bank Co., 
Ltd., the Bill on 2020 Institutional Development Plan of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the 2019 Annual Report on 
Performance Evaluation of Directors by the Board of Supervisors of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the 2019 Annual 
Report on Performance Evaluation of Supervisors by the Board of Supervisors of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., 
the 2019 Annual Report on Performance Evaluation of Senior Management by the Board of Supervisors of 
Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on Information Disclosure for the 2019 Annual Report of Laishang Bank Co., 
Ltd., the Bill on Information Disclosure for the 2019 Annual Social Responsibility Report of Laishang Bank 
Co., Ltd., and the Bill on the Amount of Proposed Cancellation of Non-performing Loans in 2020 of Laishang 
Bank Co., Ltd.On January 14, 2020, the First Interim Shareholders' General Meeting of 2020 was held in the meeting 
room on the six floor of the comprehensive business building of the Company. 43 shareholders and authorized 
agents attended the meeting, representing 2,621,753,452 shares, accounting for 87.39% of the Company's 
total share capital. The Shareholders' General Meeting has deliberated and adopted the Bill on Modifying 
Articles of Association of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on the Authorization for the Board of Directors by 
Shareholders' General Meeting of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on Increasing Shares of Henan Fangcheng 
Fengyu Village Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on Increasing Shares of Wutai Laishang Village Bank Co. Ltd., the 
Report on the Implementation of Insider and Shareholder-related Transactions in the Third Quarter of 2019 of 
Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., and the Report on Risk Management in the Third Quarter of 2019 of Laishang Bank 
Co., Ltd.On December 9, 2020, the Second Interim Shareholders' General Meeting of 2020 was held in the meeting 
room on the six floor of the comprehensive business building of the Company. 43 shareholders and authorized 
agents attended the meeting, representing 2,714,574,900 shares, accounting for 90.49% of the Company's 
total share capital. The Shareholders' General Meeting has deliberated and adopted the Bill on Management 
Measures for Related Transactions of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on the Capital Plan (2021-2023) of 
Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on Issuing Tier 2 Capital Bonds of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on 
Changing the Name of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on Modifying Articles of Association of Laishang 
Bank Co., Ltd., the Bill on Application for Resignation of Director Duan Wei, the Bill on the Election of Wang 
Jun as the Director of the Fifth Board of Directors, the Bill on the Adjustment of Business Objectives in 2020, 
the Bill on the Amount Addition of the Proposed Cancellation of Non-performing Loans in 2020, the Bill on 
the Renewal of Zhongxinghua Certified Public Accountants LLP as an External Audit Institution, the Report on 
the Implementation of Insider and Shareholder-related Transactions in the Third Quarter of 2020 of Laishang 
Bank Co., Ltd., and the Report on Risk Management in the Third Quarter of 2020 of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd.75第七章  董事会报告
一、2020年度主要经营管理情况
2020年，面对复杂多变的外部环境，公司董事会在广大股东的大力支持和监事会的监督指导
下，严格按照《公司法》《商业银行公司治理指引》等法律法规及监管要求，认真勤勉履职，实现
了规模、效益、质量的稳步提升。截至2020年12月31日，公司资产总额1540.8亿元，各项存款余额
1126.9亿元，各项贷款余额893.8亿元，实现拨备前利润（税前）20.7亿元，不良贷款率较年初下降
0.51个百分点，各项业务继续实现高质量稳健发展。
（一）规范治理机制，持续提升公司治理水平
1.规范召集召开会议。报告期内，董事会共召开6次会议，审议通过议案72项，对聘任高级管
理人员、关联企业授信、资本规划、修改章程等重大事项进行了决策。召集了3次股东大会，审议
通过议案33项，对财务决算及预算报告、风险管理报告、董监高人员的履职评价等事项进行了审
议。
2.积极发挥各专门委员会的作用。2020年，累计召开专门委员会会议25次，审议通过议案75
项。各专门委员会均制定了年度工作计划并依法合规召开会议，持续发挥委员的专业优势，向董事
会提供专业意见，切实发挥决策参谋作用，提高了董事会决策的科学性和效率性。
3.不断加强董事履职能力。2020年，董事勤勉尽职，积极履行董事职责，在会议前认真审阅
议案，按时出席会议，在表决重大事项或其他对公司有重大影响的事项时，审慎决策，切实维护了
公司和广大投资者的利益。实地到菏泽分行、泰安分行、济南分行、河南方城凤裕村镇银行及部分
网点进行调研，详细了解各机构经营发展情况，积极为各机构发展建言献策，为更好地参与公司治
理、指导经营管理奠定了良好基础。
4.完善公司治理制度体系。修订完善《莱商银行股份有限公司关联交易管理办法》，制定《莱
商银行股份有限公司股权托管办法》，完善了股权和关联交易管理制度体系，为进一步规范股权及
关联交易管理打下了坚实基础。制定《莱商银行股权投资管理办法》，进一步加强对各类被投资机
构的管理，逐步完善公司对被投资机构的管理体系。
5.将党委的核心领导作用有机融入公司治理。根据中国银保监会《健全银行业保险业公司治理
三年行动方案》和国资委要求，制定和完善了《莱商银行党委研究决定事项清单、前置研究讨论事
项清单及负面清单》，进一步明确了党委前置研究事项范围，切实发挥党委在公司治理中“把方
向、管大局、促落实”的作用。
6.加强股权管理，规范股东行为。2020年，公司向主要股东发函告知银保监会关于股权监管的
相关要求、重大违法违规股东名单和案例，强化主要股东的履职履约意识。董事会对主要股东2019
年度的履职履约情况进行了专项评估，通过股东信息核查、绘制股权关系图谱等方式，掌握主要股
东及其控股股东、实际控制人、关联方、一致行动人、最终受益人等信息，全面梳理股东行为，切76实维护股东权益。
7.及时准确披露相关信息。报告期内，公司严格按照监管要求，履行信息披露义务，加强信息
披露的主动性、针对性和有效性，高质量完成2019年度报告、2020年上半年报告的编制与披露工
作。首次披露社会责任报告，从普惠金融、绿色信贷、员工关爱、公益捐助等方面展现了公司的良
好品牌形象。相关会议通知和决议均按照规定，在公司网站和《济南日报》及时公告，保证了会议
程序的合法性和有效性。（二）发挥战略决策职能，引领全行全方位发展
1.科学制定中长期发展战略。董事会结合《国民经济和社会发展第十四个五年规划和2035年远
景目标纲要》内容及公司发展实际，对《莱商银行股份有限公司发展规划（2021-2025）》提出了
指导性意见和实施建议，进一步明确了“四步走”战略的实施路径及业务发展的目标，为实现下一
个五年宏伟蓝图和实现莱商事业“第二曲线”的新跨越奠定了框架基础。
2.创新引领业务转型发展。加大金融科技引进运用，努力构建传统业务动能升级、新兴业务全
面发力，线上、线下协同服务的发展模式，实现“传统业务+新兴业务”双轮驱动，推动经营业绩
全面提升。梳理产品与服务创新的推动、决策和管理机制，规范创新规划、协调和监督流程，完善
创新统筹管理与评估框架，创新标准更加明确、流程更加规范高效。不断丰富业务营销与服务手
段，降低经营成本，提高工作效率。
3.加强分支机构和投资机构管理。制定《2020年度机构发展规划》，持续稳步推进机构发展工
作，在济南自贸区、济阳开设传统支行，有效提升了公司在济南的市场影响力和品牌知名度。全面
梳理公司对村镇银行等被投资单位的管理流程，充分发挥公司作为主发起行和大股东在支持村镇银
行发展方面的作用，帮助村镇银行实现稳健可持续发展。
（三）强化资本管理，提升资本管理精细化水平
1.完成一级资本补充。按照董事会和股东大会决议，在全国银行间市场成功发行20亿元无固定
期限资本债券，优化了公司资本结构，增强了服务实体经济和抵御风险的能力，保障了各项业务稳
健增长。
2.组织实施内部资本充足评估。从治理及政策体系、风险偏好、压力测试、资本规划等方面，
充分考虑资产负债规模扩张速度和资本可获得性等因素，扎实开展2019年度内部资本充足评估和压
力测试工作，对各类主要风险管理状况、年度风险偏好及风险限额的执行情况、公司面临的各类实
质性风险及其对资本充足状况的影响等方面进行评估，确保公司资本充足率持续满足监管要求。
3.强化资本约束力度。积极贯彻资本精细化管理理念，督促高管层强化资本约束，鼓励发展轻资
本型业务，降低高资本消耗型资产占比，切实发挥资本管理对业务的支撑和引导作用。指导高管层合
理确定资产规模增速，合理控制表外风险资产增长，确保资本规模与公司经营管理水平相匹配。
（四）提升风险防控能力，健全合规内控机制
1.强化全面风险管理体系建设。制定2020年度风险偏好策略，明确全行风险偏好及各类风险管
理策略，科学设置资本、收益、风险等3大类33项容忍度指标，使其更加符合公司实际。建立完善77全面风险管理指标监测体系，涵盖信用风险、市场风险等9大类53项风险指标，并设定监测阈值及
频率，全面掌握各类风险水平。
2.持续巩固资产质量攻坚“334”战略成果。持续完善不良处置制度体系，修订《莱商银行抵
债资产管理办法》等8项制度，进一步夯实资产质量攻坚基础，着力提升不良资产处置质效。通过
市场卖断、推进政府支持政策落地、加大司法追偿力度等方式积极拓宽不良资产处置渠道，加快表
内外不良资产处置进度。
3.着力提升内控合规管理水平。以“完善内控管理机制、健全内控管理体系、实现内控措施有
效运行”为目标，扎实开展年度内部控制评价工作，完善内部控制体系，不断提升内控管理质效。
强化员工行为排查，利用内审系统筛选可疑数据、逐条核实，及时消除各类违规违纪苗头和风险隐
患。深化合规建设，组织开展“合规文化深化年”“行业规范建设深化年”活动，持续推进合规制
度、合规执行、合规监督、合规整纠等环节建设，努力构建“令行禁止、照章办事、主动合规、知
行合一”的合规文化。
4.规范关联交易管理。根据监管要求，开展信贷系统关联交易模块改造工作，增加关联方管
理、关联方限额管理、关联交易管理、查询统计等功能，规范了关联交易的管理流程。对行内关联
方、关联关系图谱、金融产品、授信及非授信类关联交易进行梳理，确保关联交易管理及相关指标
符合监管要求。
5.充分发挥内部审计作用。定期听取内部审计工作报告，要求内审部门坚持问题导向、目标导
向和结果导向，扎实推进年度审计计划落地，高质量完成各项审计工作。督促高级管理层对外部检
查和内部审计发现的问题进行整改，提升信息科技对审计的支撑作用，促进审计在事前风险识别与
风险规避方面发挥积极作用，充分发挥“第三道防线”的职能。 
（五）积极履行社会责任，展现良好的企业形象
1.普惠金融精准发力。制定《莱商银行央行资金复工复产专项贷款操作规程》《疫情防控期间
延期还款操作细则》等办法，明确工作标准，细化配套措施，通过扩大无还本续贷范围、增加续贷
次数、简化业务流程等措施，全力推动政策落地落实。充分发挥金融主体优势，专门申请国开行1
亿元扶贫转贷款，加大扶贫贷款的投放力度。开展“百行进万企”、首贷培植行动等专项活动，以
精准的扶持政策助力企业发展。
2.扎实开展消费者权益保护工作。修订完善《莱商银行个人金融信息保护管理办法》《莱商银
行客户投诉管理办法》，提高客户投诉处理和服务效率，提升客户满意度，切实将个人金融信息保
护工作落到实处。积极开展“金融知识万里行”“金融知识普及月”“存款保险标识启用”等宣传
活动，提高消费者的金融素养，努力践行社会责任。
3.以人为本关爱员工工作生活。打通员工“管理、专业双通道”的职业发展路径，组织开展高
级专业技术人员答辩，稳妥、有效完成专业技术人员定级、调薪工作。制定《关心关爱干部  开展
“向组织说说心里话”专项活动方案》，组织开展谈心谈话活动，加强对干部的关心关爱。建立校
招员工双导师工作机制，为每位校招员工指定业务和思想双导师，并定期进行评估和反馈，引导新
员工健康、快速成长。开展困难职工帮扶，有效减轻困难职工负担，年内划拨互助金5.5万元，帮扶78困难职工18名。
4.积极参与社会公益活动。新冠疫情防控期间，对接济南慈善总会，完成首期捐款200万元，
并在全行发起抗击疫情捐款倡议，捐款金额28.07万元，以实际行动践行责任与担当。积极参加
“莱商行·学子情”希望工程圆梦行动、“春蕾计划”、济南市东西部扶贫协作等工作，共捐助
65.8万元，有效提升了公司社会形象。

及其关联企业综合授信的议案》《关于新汶矿业集团有限责任公司及其关联企业综合授信的议案》

时股东大会的议案》。
2020年12月29日，召开第五届董事会第八次会议，审议通过了《关于召开临时董事会会议并
豁免会议通知期限的议案》《关于朱鸣董事申请辞职的议案》《关于解聘朱鸣莱商银行行长职务的
议案》《关于董事长岳隆杰代为履行行长职责的议案》。
三、2021年董事会工作计划
（一）工作思路
以党的十九大精神和习近平新时代中国特色社会主义思想为指导，按照董事会“一个中心、
两个坚持、三个提升、四个加强”的战略部署，高举高质量稳健发展大旗，继续坚持“稳中求进”
的总基调，实施“党建统领、改革提质、创新提效、管理提速”四轮驱动，以“对公做精、零售做
大、数银起跑、敏捷起步”为着力点，启动“敏捷组织建设年”，全面对标先进、全面转型创新、
全面提升能力、全面重塑形象，着力打造客户放心满意的“敏捷银行、快乐银行、清廉银行、价值
银行”。
（二）工作目标
1.确保资本充足率达到监管要求；
2.存款总额达到1254亿元，同比增长127亿元，增幅11.3%，存款偏离度符合监管要求；
3.贷款总额达到989亿元，同比增长95亿元，增幅10.6%；
4.实现净利润6.6亿元；
5.不良贷款率控制在2.0%以内，拨备覆盖率在150%以上，拨贷比达到2.5%以上；806.实现全年安全营运，无道德案件和重大责任案件发生。
（三）工作重点
1.持续完善公司治理。持续强化党建引领，不断加强各个治理主体之间的有效制衡和协调运
作，打造良好的治理文化、完善的治理机制和科学的治理体系。加强董事会建设，强化董事会对股
权管理、战略管理、全面风险管理、资本管理等重点领域的最终责任。进一步加强股东、股权及关
联方管理，维护股东合法权益。结合银保监会修订的公司治理监管新规，进一步梳理完善公司治理
制度体系，确保符合监管规定。
2.扎实推动战略规划落地实施。稳步推进“四步走”战略实施，加强与相关部门的汇报沟通，
密切关注外部舆情与监管动态，确保“四步走”规划平稳有序推进。细化战略规划的实施路径，分
区域、分条线、分部门进行目标任务分解，明确战略规划落地实施的责任部门、具体措施和工作方
向。建立完善后评估机制，在落地过程中及时纠偏，确保战略落地实施效果。
3.严守风险防控底线。制定与发展战略相匹配的风险偏好策略，完善风险偏好传导机制及运行
监测体系，逐步构建全行统一的风险管理视图。建设更加完善的合规管理架构，丰富合规管理的工
具，深入推进涵盖各个风险点的合规管理体系建设，为全行合规经营、规范管理保驾护航。加强资
产质量管控，严格客户准入管理，强化风险排查预警，严防不良反弹。
4.强化资本规划和管理。进一步完善资本管理的顶层设计，推动增资扩股和25亿二级资本债券
发行工作，优化资本结构，增强资本实力，支持业务增长和战略规划的实施，实现协调和可持续发
展。根据新资本办法的要求，加强对资本计量的监测，增强资本集约化经营能力，提升资本的精细
化管理水平。
5.加快推动数字化转型。优化业务流程，按照“产品获客、社交粘合、数据赋能、分类服务”
的总体思路，整合打通营销管理中的各独立环节，建立线上化营销闭环体系。持续推进数据保护和
数据治理，完善数据管理体系，提升数据处理能力，强化数据创新应用。提高敏捷化的产品创新能
力，通过产品组合、参数化配置、定制化开发等方法，实现产品快速创新，为政府部门、核心企
业、中小微企业、商户、自然人提供高效的金融服务。
6.着力加强提升团队建设。完善新员工招聘培养体系，以完善双导师工作机制、提供展现平
台、加强转岗培训为抓手，加强新员工招聘及培训管理。通过社会招聘及时补充各类人才，建立健
全各类人才队伍，尤其是加大科技人才招聘力度，实现科技与业务的融合与发展。加强队伍建设，
落实全行人才发展战略，做好后备干部、“菁英人才”及内训师管理培训。完善人才激励机制，探
索选拔一批具有莱商工匠精神的员工，丰富激励形式，激发员工队伍活力。做好薪酬政策及管理机
制的优化调整，探索开展多样化的绩效考核方式，充分发挥绩效考核对业务发展的激励促进作用。
四、利润分配方案
风险准备 8,635,789.56元；剩余未分配利润 1,919,872,036.34元结转以后年度。2020年度计提盈余公积金58,567,942.07元，计提任意盈余公积金11,713,588.41元，提取一般81Chapter VII Report of the Board of DirectorsI. Review of Main Operation and Management in 2020In 2020, in the face of a complicated and volatile external environment and under the 
supervision and guidance of the supervisory authority, the strong support of shareholders, and 
the supervision and support of the Board of Supervisors, the Board of Directors of the Company, 
strictly following the Company Law of the People's Republic of China, Guidelines on Corporate 
Governance of Commercial Banks, and other laws and regulations and supervision requirements, 
performed its function in a serious and diligent way and promoted the high-quality and steady 
development of the bank continuously, realizing the coordinated and balanced development in scale, 
efficiency and quality. As of December 31, 2020, the Company had total assets of RMB154.08 
billion, a total deposit balance of RMB112.69 billion, a total loan balance of RMB89.38 billion, a 
pre-provision profit (before tax) of RMB2.07 billion, and a non-performing loan ratio decreased by 
0.51 percentage points compared with the beginning of the year, with the continuous high-quality 
and steady development of various businesses.(i) The Company standardized the governance mechanism and continuously 
enhanced the corporate governance level1. The Company convened and held meetings in a standardized manner. During the reporting 
period, the Board of Directors held 6 meetings in total, with 72 proposals reviewed and approved, 
in which some major issues such as the appointment of senior managers, the credit of affiliated 
companies, capital planning, and the amendment of the articles of association were decided. And it 
convened 3 general meetings of shareholders, with 33 proposals considered and approved, in which 
matters such as financial final accounts and budget reports, risk management reports, and evaluation 
of the performance of directors, supervisors and senior managers were reviewed.2. The Company actively gave play to the role of each special committee. In 2020, the Board 
of Directors held 25 special committee meetings in total, with 75 proposals reviewed and approved. 
Each special committee formulated an annual work plan and held meetings in compliance with laws 
and regulations, with their consistent professional advantages, provided opinions for the Board of 
Directors and effectively played the role of decision-making consultants, which promoted more 
scientific and efficient decision-making of the Board of Directors.3. The Company continued to strengthen the directors' ability to perform their duties. In 2020, 
the directors performed their duties diligently and actively. They carefully reviewed proposals 
before meetings and attended on time, and made prudent decisions when voting on major issues or 
other matters that had a significant impact on the Company, earnestly safeguarding the interests of 
the Company and investors. The directors went to Heze Branch, Tai'an Branch, and Jinan Branch, 
Henan Fangcheng Fengyu County Bank, and some branches to conduct investigations on the spot 
and learned more about the operation and development of each branch. By this, they actively put82forward suggestions for the development of each branch, and laid a solid foundation for them to 
better participate in corporate governance and guidance on business operation and management.4. The Company perfected the governance system. The Company, amended the Management 
Measures for Related Party Transactions of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd. and formulated the Measures 
for Equity Trust of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., which perfected the equity and related-party transaction 
management system and laid a solid foundation for the next step to standardize the management. 
And the Company formulated the Management Measures for Equity Investment of Laishang Bank 
Co., Ltd., further strengthening the management of various invested institutions, and gradually 
improving the management system for those institutions.5. The company organically integrated the core leading role of the Party committee into the 
corporate governance. In accordance with the Three-year Action Plan for Improving Corporate 
Governance of Banking and Insurance Industry by China Banking and Insurance Regulatory 
Commission and the requirements of the SASAC, the Company formulated and perfected the List 
of Research Decisions, List of Pre-Research and Discussion Items, and Negative List of the Party 
Committee of Laishang Bank, which further clarified the scope of Party committee's pre-research 
items. The role of the Party committee in "controlling the direction, managing the overall situation 
and promoting the implementation" in corporate governance had been brought into full play.6. The Company strengthened equity management and regulated shareholders' behavior. In 
2020, the Company sent a letter to the major shareholders to inform them the relevant requirements 
for equity supervision of the China Banking and Insurance Regulatory Commission and the list of 
shareholders in major violation of laws and regulations and cases, which strengthened the major 
shareholders' awareness to perform their duties and implement the conventions. The Board of 
Directors conducted a special assessment of the performance of the major shareholders in 2019. And 
through the shareholder information verification and drawing equity relationship map, the Board 
of Directors fully learned about such information as the major shareholders and their controlling 
shareholders, actual controllers, related parties, persons acting in concert, and ultimate beneficiaries, 
comprehensively sorted out the behavior of shareholders, and effectively protected their rights and 
interests.7. The Company disclosed relevant information in a timely and accurate manner. During the 
reporting period, the company performed information disclosure obligations strictly following the 
regulatory requirements. It strengthened the initiative, pertinence and effectiveness of information 
disclosure, and completed the preparation and disclosure of the 2019 annual report and the 2020 
first half report with high quality. The first disclosure of the social responsibility report, in terms 
of financial inclusion, green credit, employee care, charity donations, etc., reflected the Company's 
good brand image. The notices and resolutions of the Company's meetings were announced on the 
Company's website and Jinan Daily in a timely manner in accordance with regulations, ensuring the 
legality and effectiveness of the meeting procedures.(ii) The Company gave play to the function of strategic decision-making and 
led the all-round development of the bank1. The Company scientifically formulated the medium and long-term development strategies.83Combining the content of the “Outline of 14th Five-Year Plan for National Economic and Social 
Development and Long-Term Goals for 2035” with the actual development of the Company, the 
Board of Directors put forward guiding opinions and implementation suggestions on the Development 
Plan of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd. (2021-2025), further clarified the implementation approach of 
the "Four Steps" strategy and goal of business development, and laid a framework foundation for 
realizing the grand blueprint for next five years and realizing the new leap of the “Second Curve” of 
Laishang Bank's business.2. The company led business transformation and development through innovation. The 
company increased the introduction and application of financial technology, strived to build a 
development mode of upgrading traditional business growth drivers, promoting emerging business 
fully into action and serving cooperatively online and offline, realized the dual wheel drive of 
"traditional business + emerging business", and promoted the comprehensive improvement of 
business performance. And also, the company sorted out the promotion, decision-making and 
management mechanism of product and service innovation, standardized the planning, coordination 
and supervision process of innovation, improved the innovation overall management and evaluation 
framework, and made the innovation standard clearer and the process more standardized and 
efficient. Meanwhile, the Company constantly enriched business marketing and service means, 
reduced operating costs and improved work efficiency.3. The Company strengthened the management of branches and invested institutions. The 
Company formulated the 2020 Institutional Development Plan, continuously and steadily promoted 
institutional development, and opened traditional branches in Jinan Free Trade Zone and Jiyang, 
which effectively increased the Company's market influence and brand awareness in Jinan. The 
Company comprehensively sorted out the management process to the village banks and other 
invested institutions, and gave full play to the role of the company as the main initiating bank and 
major shareholder in supporting the development of the village banks, so as to help the village banks 
achieve stable and sustainable development.(iii) The Company strengthened capital management and enhanced the level 
of fine capital management1. The Company completed tier one capital replenishment. In accordance with the resolutions of 
the Board of Directors and the general meetings of shareholders, the Company successfully issued 
RMB 2 billion of non-fixed-term capital bonds in the national inter-bank market, The successful 
issuance of non-fixed-term capital bonds optimized the capital structure, enhanced the ability to 
serve the real economy and resist risks, and ensured the steady growth of various businesses.2. The Company organized and implemented the assessment of internal capital adequacy. From 
the aspects of governance and policy system, risk preference, stress test, capital planning, etc., fully 
considering factors including scale expansion speed of assets and liabilities and capital availability, 
the Company solidly carried out the internal capital adequacy assessment and stress test in 2019, 
and evaluated the main risk management status, annual risk preference and implementation of risk 
limits, various substantive risks faced by the company and its impact on capital adequacy, so as to 
ensure that the company's capital adequacy ratio continues to meet regulatory requirements.843. The Company strengthened capital constraint. The Company actively implemented the 
fine capital management concept, urged the senior management to strengthen capital constraint, 
encouraged the development of light capital business, reduced the proportion of assets with high 
capital consumption, and practically gave play to the roles of support and guidance of capital 
management for businesses. The Company guided the senior management to reasonably determined 
the growth rate of the asset scale, reasonably controlled the growth of off-balance-sheet risky assets, 
and ensured that the capital scale matched the operation and management level of the Company.(iv) The Company improved risk prevention and control capabilities and 
improved compliance and internal control mechanisms1. The Company strengthened the construction of a comprehensive risk management system. 
The Company formulated the 2020 risk preference strategy, clarified the risk preference and 
various risk management strategies of the bank, scientifically set up 33 tolerance indicators in 3 
categories of capital, revenue and risk, and made the indicators comply with the actual situation of 
the Company. The Company established and improved a comprehensive risk management indicator 
monitoring system, covering 53 risk indicators in 9 categories of credit risk and market risk, and set 
up monitoring thresholds and frequencies to fully understand various risk levels.2. The company constantly consolidated the achievements of the “334” strategy for asset 
quality. The Company continued to improve the non-performing assets disposal system, revised 8 
systems including the Measures for the Administration of Debt-expiated Assets in Laishang Bank, 
further consolidated the foundation for asset quality, and strove to improve the quality and efficiency 
of non-performing assets disposal. The Company actively expanded the channel of non-performing 
assets disposal, and accelerated the progress of on and off-balance-sheet non-performing assets 
disposal by means of market-based outright sale, promoting the implementation of government 
supporting policies, increasing judicial recovery efforts and etc.3. The Company strived to enhance the internal control and compliance management level. 
The Company, taking "the perfection and improvement of the internal control management system 
and the effective implement of the internal control measures" as orientation, solidly carried out the 
annual internal control evaluation, improved the internal control system and continued to increase 
the quality and efficiency of internal control management. The Company strengthened the employee 
behavior investigation, and used the internal audit system to screen and verify suspicious data one by 
one to timely eliminate all kinds of violations of regulations and disciplines and potential risks. The 
Company deepened compliance, organized some activities such as "Compliance Culture Deepening 
Year" and "Construction of Industry Standards Deepening Year", promoted the construction 
of compliance regulation, compliance performing, compliance supervision, and compliance 
rectification and other links, and strove to build a compliance culture of "strict enforcement of orders 
and prohibitions, action according to the rules, active compliance and unity of knowing and doing".4. The Company standardized the related party transaction management. According to the 
regulatory requirements, the Company carried out related party transaction module renovation for 
the credit management system, increased some functions, such as the management of related parties, 
limits management of related parties, related party transaction management, and query statistics,85which standardized the related party transaction management procedures. The Company sorted 
out intra-bank related parties, association spectrum, financial products, and credit and non-credit 
related party transactions, so as to ensure that the related party transaction management and relevant 
indicators meet the regulatory requirements.5. The Company gave full play to the role of internal audit. The Board of Directors regularly 
listened to the work report on the internal audit. The internal audit department was required to adhere 
to problem-oriented, goal-oriented and result-oriented approach, push forward the implementation of 
the annual audit plan, and complete all audit work with high quality. The Board of Directors urged 
senior management to rectify the problems found in external inspection and internal audit, enhanced 
the role of Information Technology in supporting audit, promoted audit to play a positive role in pre-
risk identification and risk avoidance, and give full play to the function of "the third line of defense".(v) The Company fulfilled social responsibility actively and showed a good 
corporate image1. The Company made well-targeted efforts in inclusive finance. The Company formulated the 
Operating Procedures for Special Loan of Laishang Bank from Central Bank Fund for Resumption 
of Work and Production and the Operation Rules for Deferred Repayment during Epidemic 
Prevention and Control Period, and clarified working standards, and refined supporting measures. 
The Company made every effort to promote the implementation of the policy by expanding the 
scope of non-repayment loan renewal, increasing the number of loan renewal times, simplifying 
business processes and other measures. The company gave full play to the advantages of financial 
entities, specially applied for RMB100 million of poverty alleviation loan from China Development 
Bank, and increased the supply of poverty alleviation loan. Special activities such as "Hundreds of 
Banks Connecting with Thousands Enterprises" and "first loan support" were carried out to help the 
development of enterprises with accurate supporting policies.2. The Company carried out consumer rights protection solidly. The Company revised and 
improved the Administrative Measures for the Protection of Personal Financial Information of 
Laishang Bank and the Administrative Measures for Customer Complaints of Laishang Bank, 
improved customer complaint handling and service efficiency to increase customer satisfaction, 
and promoted the implementation of personal financial information protection work. The Company 
actively carried out publicity activities, such as "Mastering Financial Knowledge to Travel around 
the World", "Financial Knowledge Popularization Month", and "Deposit Insurance Logo Opening 
Day", to improve financial literacy of consumers and practice social responsibility.3. The Company put people first and cared for the work and life of employees. The company 
opened the career development path of "double channels of management and specialty" for 
employees, organized the defense of senior professional technicians, and steadily and effectively 
completed the grading and salary adjustment of professional technicians. The Company formulated 
the Plan to Carry out the Special Activity of Talking to the Organization and Caring for Cadres and 
organized and carried out heart-to-heart talk activities to strengthen care for cadres. The Company 
established a dual mentor work mechanism for employees recruited from schools, assigned business 
and ideological mentors to each employee, and conducted regular evaluation and feedback to guide86the healthy and rapid growth of new employees. The Company carried out the assistance to workers 
in difficulty to effectively reduce the burden of difficult workers and allocated RMB55,000 of mutual 
aid funds during the year to help 18 workers.4. The Company participated in social public welfare activities actively. During COVID-19 
prevention and control, the Company donated RMB2 million to Jinan Charity Association in the 
first installation, and launched a donation initiative to fight the epidemic throughout the bank, with a 
donation amount of 280,700 Yuan, fulfilling its responsibility with practical actions. The Company 
actively participated in the "Laishang Action·Student Sentiment", a dream action of the Hope 
Project, and the "Spring Buds Program", the collaborative work on poverty alleviation in the East 
and West of Jinan, with a total amount of RMB 658,000, which effectively improved the Company's 
social image.II. Daily Work of the Board of DirectorsThe Board of Directors of the Company held six general meetings of shareholders during thereporting period, with the details as follows:On  March  12,  2020,  the  3rd  meeting  of  the  Fifth  Board  of  Directors  was  held  in  a

of President's Duties were deliberated and adopted.III. 2020 Work Plan of the Board of Directors(i) Working ideasUnder the guidance of the spirit of the 19th National Congress of the Communist Party of China 
and Xi Jinping Thought on Socialism with Chinese Characteristics for a New Era, based on the 
strategic deployment of "one-center, two-insistence, three-upgrade, and four-enhancement" of the 
Board of Directors, hold the principle of high-quality stable development, keep the overall base of 
"make progress while ensuring stability", and implement the policy of "guide by Party construction, 
quality improvement by reform, efficiency promotion by innovation, and speed increase by 
management". Focusing on "corporation business refinement, retail enlargement, digital bank 
launching, and agile start", launch the "year for agile organization construction". Follow the example 
of advanced enterprises, implement the transformation through innovation, improve the capacity, 
and create a new image comprehensively, and make efforts to develop Laishang into an "agile bank, 
happy bank, incorruptible bank, and valuable bank" meeting clients' needs.(ii)Work objectives1. Ensure that the capital adequacy ratio meets the regulatory requirements; 
2.  Ensure  the  total  deposits  to  hit  RMB125.4  billion,  representing  an  increase  of 
RMB12.7billion or 11.3% on a year-on-year basis, with the deposit deviation complying with the 
regulatory requirements;3. The total loans are planned to hit RMB98.9 billion, representing an increase of RMB9.5billion or 10.6% on a year-on-year basis;4. The net profit are planned to reach RMB 660 million; 
5. The non-performing loan ratio should be controlled within 2.0%, with the provisioningcoverage rate above 150% and the ratio of provisioning to loan above 2.5%;6. Realize safe operation and no moral case and major responsibility case throughout the year.(iii)Working priorities1. Continuously improve comporate governance. Continuously strengthen the Party construction 
leadership, strengthen the effective checks and balances and coordinated operation among various89governance subjects, and create a good governance culture, perfect governance mechanism and 
scientific governance system. Strengthen the construction of the Board of Directors, strengthen the 
final responsibility of the Board of Directors in key fields, such us equity management, strategy 
management, comprehensive risk management, capital management, etc. Further strengthen the 
management of shareholders, equities and related parties, and protect the legitimate rights and 
interests of shareholders. Combined with the new regulation rules of corporate governance revised 
by the CIRC, further sort out and improve the corporate governance system, to conform with the 
regulation rules.2.  Solidly  promote  the  implementation  of  strategy  planning.  Steadily  promote  the 
implementation of the "four-step" strategy, enhance the report and communication with relevant 
department, focus on external public opinions and regulation trends, to ensure the stable and orderly 
promotion of the "four-step" strategy. Refine the implementation route of strategy planning, break 
target tasks down in areas, in lines, and in departments, and clarify the responsible department, 
specific measures and work direction of the implementation of the strategic planning. Establish and 
improve post-evaluation system, correct the deviation in the process of implementation, and ensure 
the implementation effect of the strategy.3. Strictly adhere to the bottom line of risk prevention and control. Establish a risk preference 
strategy matching the development strategy, improve the risk preference transmission mechanism 
and operational and monitoring system, and gradually develop a risk management view applicable 
to the whole bank. Build a more perfect compliance management framework, enrich the tools of 
compliance management, and further promote the construction of compliance management system 
covering all risk points, so as to ensure the whole bank’s compliance operating and standardized 
management. Enhance the management and control of asset quality, strictly conduct client access 
management, strengthen risk investigation and early-warning, and prevent problems from rebound.4. Enhance capital planning and management. Further improve the top-level design of capital 
management, and promote the capital increase and share enlargement and the issue of tier-2 capital 
bonds worth RMB 2.5 billion. Optimize the capital structure, increase the capital strength, support 
the implementation of business growth and strategy planning, to realize coordinated and sustainable 
development. In accordance with the requirements of the new capital approach, strengthen the 
monitoring of capital measurement, improve the ability of capital-intensive operation, and enhance 
refined management level of capitals.5. Accelerate to promote digital transformation. Optimize the business process, according to 
the general idea of "Obtaining customers with products, connecting customers with social networks, 
enabling data, and servicing in different ways", integrate and open up all independent links in 
marketing management, and establish online marketing closed-loop system. Continue to promote 
data protection and data governance, improve data management system, enhance data processing 
capacity, and strengthen data innovation and application. Improve flexible product innovation 
capacity, achieve rapid product innovation through product combination, parametric configuration, 
customized development and other methods, so as to provide efficient financial services for 
government departments, core enterprises, small and medium-sized enterprises, individually-owned 
business and natural persons.6. Focus on the improvement of team construction. Improve the recruitment and cultivation90system of new employees, and strengthen the recruitment, training, and management of new 
employees through improving the double-tutor working mechanism, supporting a showing 
platform, and enhancing the position-transfer training. Timely absorb various talents through social 
recruitment, establish and improve teams of various talents, especially increase the recruitment 
of scientific and technological talents, and realize the integration and development of technology 
and business. Strengthen the team building, implement the talent development strategy of the 
whole bank, and do a good job in the management training of reserve cadres, "excellent talents" 
and internal trainers. Improve the talent incentive mechanism, explore and select employees with 
craftsmanship spirit of Laishang Bank, enrich the incentive forms, and stimulate the vitality of 
the staff. Improve and adjust salary policy and management mechanism, explore and carry out 
multiple modes for performance assessment, and bring performance into full play to promote the 
development of businesses across the bank.IV. Profit Distribution SchemeIn 2020, the surplus reserved funds withdrawn were RMB58,567,942.07, the arbitrary 
reserved funds withdrawn were RMB11,713,588.41 and the general risk reserves allotted were 
RMB8,635,789.56; the remaining undistributed profit of1,919,872,036.34 is carried over into the 
later year.91第八章 监事会报告

二、监事会就有关事项发表的独立意见 
 （一）公司依法经营情况 
报告期内，公司坚持依法、合规经营，规范管理，经营决策程序符合法律、法规及公司章程
的有关规定，董事及高级管理人员在业务经营及管理过程中谨慎、认真、勤勉，未发现违法违规
行为和损害公司、股东利益行为。
（二）财务报告真实性
2019年度财务报告已由中兴华会计师事务所根据《企业会计制度》和《企业会计准则》有关
规定进行审计，并出具标准无保留意见审计报告。财务报告真实、客观、公允地反映了公司的财
务状况和经营成果。
（三）关联交易情况
公司的关联交易主要是股东贷款。监事会认为，报告期内，公司在处理关联交易时，严格遵
守有关规定，履行关联交易操作程序，交易过程体现了公平合理原则，关联交易符合商业原则，93未发现损害股东权益和公司利益的行为。
（四）内部控制制度情况监事会听取和审阅了《公司2019年度内部控制评价报告》，认为公司制定了较为完整、合理、有效的内部控制制度。（五）股东大会决议执行情况
监事会对董事会提交股东大会审议的各项报告和提案进行了查阅和调研，没有异议。监事会
对股东大会决议的执行情况进行了监督，认为董事会按照公司治理要求，认真执行了股东大会的
有关决议。94Chapter VIII Report of the Board of SupervisorsI. Meetings held by the Board of Supervisors in 2020

deliberated and adopted.II.  Independent  Opinions  on  Relevant  Issues  from  the  Board  of96Supervisors
(i) Legal Operation of the CompanyDuring the reporting period, the Company has stuck to operation in accordance with laws 
and regulations and normalization of the management. The decision-making procedure met the 
related provisions of laws, regulations and the Articles of Association. The directors and the senior 
management were able to conscientiously implement their duties. No director or senior management 
has been discovered to have breached any laws or regulations or Articles of Association or harmed 
the interest of the Company when they execute their functions.
(ii)   Authenticity of Financial ReportsZhongxinghua Certified Public Accountants LLP has carefully audited the 2019 Annual 
Financial Report in accordance with Accounting System for Enterprises and Accounting Standard 
for Enterprises and issued a standard unqualified audit report. The financial report has truthfully and 
fairly reflected the Company's financial position and operation results.
(iii) The Related TransactionsThe related transactions of the Company are mainly shareholders' loans. The Board of 
Supervisors thinks that during the reporting period when dealing with related transactions, the 
Company has strictly observed related regulations and performed the operating procedure of related 
transactions. Transaction processes have reflected the principle of fairness and justifiableness. The 
related transactions meet the commercial principles and no action compromising the interests of the 
Company or shareholders has been discovered.
(iv) The Internal Control SystemThe Board of Supervisors heard and deliberated the 2019 Annual Internal Control Report of 
Laishang Bank Co., Ltd., and believed that the Company has formulated the relatively complete, 
reasonable and effective internal control system.
(v) Implementation of the Resolutions Approved in the Shareholders' General 
MeetingsThe Board of Supervisors has reviewed and investigated all reports and proposals submitted by 
the Board of Directors to the Shareholders' General Meeting for deliberation, without any objection. 
The Board of Supervisors has supervised over the implementation of the resolutions approved at 
the shareholders' general meetings, and thinks that the Board of Directors of the Company is able to 
conscientiously implement the related resolutions of the shareholders' general meetings according to 
the requirements of corporate governance.97第九章 重要事项

Major Fund Raising of the CompanyOn August 19, 2020, the company issued write-down non-fixed-term capital bonds worth2,000,000,000 yuan.
IV. The Company's Employment and Dismissal of CPAsIn 2020, the Company employed Zhongxinghua Certified Public Accountants LLP to audit the2019 financial statements of the Company.
V. Major Litigation and ArbitrationDuring the reporting period, there was no major litigation and arbitration in the Company. By 
December 31, 2020, there were 633 lawsuits in the Company. The major litigation of the Company 
are actively filed for recovering the non-performing loans. The Company thinks, the major litigation  
of the Company do not constitute any significant adverse effect on the financial conditions or 
operating results of the Company.

O.4第十一章  备查文件
一、载有公司董事长签名的年度报告正本；
二、载有法定代表人、行长、财务负责人签字并盖章的会计报表；
三、2020年度审计报告及财务报表附注；
四、《莱商银行股份有限公司章程》Chapter XI  Documents Available for InspectionI. The original annual report with signature of the Chairman of the 
Company;II. The financial statements with signatures of the legal representative, 
President  and  Finance  Director  of  the  Company  and  seal  of  the 
Company;III.The 2020 annual audit report and the notes to financial statements;IV.Articles of Association of Laishang Bank Co., Ltd.112
